Universal Ad Laws Compliance

✓Law 1: Headline IS the ad (mapped to Tiana formulas)
✓Law 2: Sell the destination, not the flight
✓Law 3: 0.5-second hook test
✓Law 4: ONE emotion per ad
✓Law 5: Customer language (from BiggerPockets, Trustpilot, BBB)
✓Law 6: Research first, create second (10-tab Suby)
✓Law 7: Every line earns its place
✓Law 8: No new objections raised
✓Law 10: Hooks tested first (5 per angle)
✓Law 12: The guarantee IS the offer (replacement guarantee)
✓Law 13: ONE belief (verified data = more connections)
✓Law 16: Industry language (skip trace, DNC, connect rate)
✓Law 17: Andromeda signals (HOMEOWNER DATA eyebrow)
✓Law 21: 2-4 words scroll-stop
✓Law 23: Cheeky filter: sales floor humor (male 25-45)
✓Law 24: Decision maker = ops director or owner
✓Law 25: Typography prescribed in prompts
✓Law 28: Real urgency (cost-of-delay per angle)
✓Law 29: Permission CTAs (You can...)
✓Law 30: Curiosity gap preservation

Dead Numbers? Gone.
Every bad number replaced free. No limit.
View Full Ad Copy
What percentage of your phone list actually picks up? Javier found out the hard way. Runs a two-person wholesaling operation out of Houston. Spent $500 on a skip trace list. Sat down at 9am with coffee and a script he'd practiced in the mirror. ❌ By noon, he'd dialed 247 numbers. 83 were disconnected. 41 went to people who'd never heard of the property. One woman yelled at him in Spanish. His exact words on BiggerPockets: "It's been 2 or 3 hours I've been calling this list and it's riddled with dead numbers." 🚨 That's not a hustle problem. That's a data problem — and it's the same data everyone's selling. ✅ We verify every number before delivery. The ones that slip through? Replaced free. No limit. No questions. ⚡ While you're reading this, your team is dialing from that same unverified list. 💰 Every hour is another $200+ in payroll spent talking to nobody. ❌ That cost doesn't pause while you think about it. 👉 You can see what a verified list looks like for your market — takes about 60 seconds to build a sample.

FORMAT: 1080x1920 (9:16 vertical) | 15 seconds | 30fps
COLOR GRADE: High-contrast noir. Blacks crushed to #0a0a0a. Desaturated scenes 1-2, color blooms in scene 3.
MUSIC: Low tension drone (scenes 1-2) -> clean piano resolution (scenes 3-4).

SCENE 1 (0-3s): HOOK — QUESTION SLAM
- Black screen (#000000). 0.5s hold.
- At 0.5s: "Dead Numbers?" appears — DM Serif Display, 96pt, white (#ffffff), center-screen.
- At 1.5s: Text glitches (RGB split, 4px offset, 3 frames) then snaps to red (#ef4444).
- At 2.0s: "Gone." slams in below — DM Serif Display, 120pt, green (#22c55e), screen-shake (3px, 4 frames).
- At 2.5s: Thin horizontal line (#2563eb, 2px) draws left-to-right beneath "Gone."
- Sound: Deep bass hit on "Dead Numbers?" — sharp metallic clang on "Gone."

SCENE 2 (3-7s): AGITATE — PHONE GRAVEYARD
- Dissolve to phone screen mockup (dark UI, centered, 60% width).
- Contact list scrolls upward. Each entry has:
  - Redacted name bar (gray #64748b)
  - Status rotating: "Disconnected" (red #ef4444), "Wrong Number" (orange #f59e0b), "Not in Service" (#b91c1c)
  - Small red X icon next to each
- Counter overlay top-right: "Dead: 1... 14... 31... 47..." Inter Mono, 28pt, red (#ef4444).
- At 5.5s: Counter freezes at "Dead: 347 / 500"
- Text overlay bottom-third: "You're paying for all 500." — Inter 600, 22pt, white.
- Sound: Rapid-fire disconnected tones (boop-boop-boop). Cash register on each tick.

SCENE 3 (7-11s): PROOF — CLEAN SWEEP
- Hard cut. Navy background (#0f172a).
- Verified data card slides in from bottom — white card, rounded corners (16px), subtle shadow.
- Card header: green checkmark + "VERIFIED RECORD" Inter 700, 14pt, green (#22c55e).
- Fields populate one by one with blue glow animation (0.3s each):
  - "Phone: Active" (green dot) | "Alt Phone: Active" | "Email: Deliverable"
  - "Home Value: $285,000" | "Mortgage: 78% LTV" | "DNC: Clear"
- Text overlay: "Every dead number replaced. Free." — DM Serif Display, 36pt, white.
- Sound: Satisfying "ding" chime on each field. Ascending synth pad.

SCENE 4 (11-15s): CTA — BRAND CARD
- Smooth zoom-out to full brand layout on navy (#0f172a).
- "BookedSolid Pro" logo centered — white with blue (#2563eb) diamond, 48pt.
- Below: "Verified data. Dead numbers replaced." — Inter 500, 22pt, #94a3b8.
- CTA pill: blue (#2563eb) rounded rectangle, "Build a Free List" white Inter 700, 20pt. Pulse animation.
- Below pill: "60 seconds. No credit card." — Inter 400, 14pt, #64748b.

Have you ever wondered why 4 out of 10 numbers on your homeowner list just... ring into nothing? It's not bad luck. And it's not your dialer. There's a reason nobody in the skip trace industry talks about this publicly. Here's what actually happens behind the scenes: Most list providers pull from the same 3-4 aggregated databases. Those databases update quarterly — sometimes less. In between updates, people move, change carriers, port numbers, or disconnect entirely. By the time that CSV hits your inbox, a huge chunk of it is already dead. 🚨 They know this when they sell it to you. The industry profit model depends on volume, not accuracy. Sell 10,000 records at $0.04 each, move on. Whether 3,800 of those numbers actually work? Not their problem. 👀 "I've been through 3 providers. Same dead numbers, same databases, same excuses." — Marcus T., BiggerPockets ❌ No verification layer before delivery ❌ No accountability for disconnected numbers ❌ No replacement when half the list is dead ✅ We verify every number before it ships ✅ Every bad number gets replaced free — no cap ✅ 18+ data points per record including DNC status ✅ TCPA compliance flags built in 🔥 The entire model is built on one idea: you shouldn't pay for data that doesn't connect. 👉 While your team dials through yesterday's data, someone in your market is reaching the same homeowners first — because their list was verified this week. You can see what a verified list looks like for your zip codes. Takes about 60 seconds to pull a sample.

Nobody told you the real problem: the data was already dead before you downloaded it. 🚨 Here's the dirty secret of skip tracing: most providers pull from databases that update once a quarter. Some update twice a year. In between? People move. Carriers recycle numbers. Homeowners port to new phones. By the time your team sits down on Monday morning, 30-50% of those numbers have already expired. Not because the provider made a mistake — because that's how the system was built. Still Buying Skip Traces Blind?
Ask one question. Change everything.
View Full Ad Copy
Real estate investors still buying skip traces blind — this is for you. If you're pulling homeowner lists for cold calling and you've never asked your provider how often their database updates — you need to read this. Because the answer is probably going to make you uncomfortable. 👉 Most providers aggregate from the same 3-4 national databases. Those databases update quarterly at best. Some update twice a year. In between, roughly 38% of phone numbers go stale — carriers recycle them, homeowners switch, numbers get ported or disconnected. Nobody tells you this at checkout. You see a per-record price, you see a record count, you download a CSV. What you don't see is the timestamp on that data — or the disconnect rate baked into it. 👀 “I just got 1000 numbers for calling. About 300-400 of them are already disconnected. Is that normal?” — Real post, BiggerPockets forum, 2024 ❌ No verification between database and delivery ❌ No transparency on data freshness ❌ No accountability for disconnected numbers ❌ No replacement policy Here's one question that changes everything: “Do you verify each number before delivery, and what happens if it's wrong?” If your provider can't answer both parts clearly, you already have your answer. ✅ We verify every number before it ships ✅ Every bad number replaced free — no limit ✅ 18+ data points per record including DNC and TCPA compliance ✅ Replacement guarantee aligns our profit with your connect rate 🔥 The question isn't whether you can afford verified data. It's whether you can keep paying for data that doesn't connect. ➡️ You can check what verified data looks like for your zip codes — takes about 60 seconds to pull a sample.

Have you ever wondered why 4 out of 10 numbers on your homeowner list just... ring into nothing? It's not bad luck. And it's not your dialer. There's a reason nobody in the skip trace industry talks about this publicly. Here's what actually happens behind the scenes: Most list providers pull from the same 3-4 aggregated databases. Those databases update quarterly — sometimes less. In between updates, people move, change carriers, port numbers, or disconnect entirely. By the time that CSV hits your inbox, a huge chunk of it is already dead. 🚨 They know this when they sell it to you. The industry profit model depends on volume, not accuracy. Sell 10,000 records at $0.04 each, move on. Whether 3,800 of those numbers actually work? Not their problem. 👀 "I've been through 3 providers. Same dead numbers, same databases, same excuses." — Marcus T., BiggerPockets ❌ No verification layer before delivery ❌ No accountability for disconnected numbers ❌ No replacement when half the list is dead ✅ We verify every number before it ships ✅ Every bad number gets replaced free — no cap ✅ 18+ data points per record including DNC status ✅ TCPA compliance flags built in 🔥 The entire model is built on one idea: you shouldn't pay for data that doesn't connect. 👉 While your team dials through yesterday's data, someone in your market is reaching the same homeowners first — because their list was verified this week. You can see what a verified list looks like for your zip codes. Takes about 60 seconds to pull a sample.

Homeowner picks up. 4 minutes, appointment set. - Third dial: rings. Voicemail. Move on. - Fifth dial: rings. Conversation. Homeowner is interested, books for Thursday. - By 11am, the team is ahead of pace and energy is high. Team A? By 11am, two callers had already taken an early break. That means your team is spending roughly 68% of their dial time reaching nobody. 👀 “Out of 500 records, maybe 150 were actually reachable. The rest were dead numbers or wrong people entirely.” — Brandon M., BiggerPockets 👉 Here's what 38% dead numbers actually costs you: - A 3-person call team at $200/day each = $600/day - 68% wasted = $408/day paying people to listen to disconnected tones - That's $2,040/week in payroll burned on dead data - $8,160/month. Before you count the deals you missed. ❌ No verification before delivery ❌ No replacement for dead numbers ❌ No transparency on disconnect rates ✅ We verify every number before it reaches your team ✅ Every bad number replaced free — unlimited ✅ 18+ data points per record including DNC status and TCPA flags ✅ Replacement guarantee so the economics work in your favor 🔥 $8,160/month is the cost of not knowing this number.
